Estádio Municipal Coaracy da Mata Fonseca, Arapiraca, is a multi-use stadium in Arapiraca, Brazil. It is currently used mostly for football matches and hosts the home matches of Arapiraquense. The stadium has a capacity of 6,799 people.

The Bootleg Series Volume 1: The Quine Tapes is an album by The Velvet Underground. It has a runtime of 230.05 and was recorded in United States. The genre of the album is Rock music. The album was produced by The Velvet Underground and was recorded in St. Louis, Missouri. It was released by Polydor Records.
The Fellowship of the Ring was first published on 29 July 1954 and is the first of three volumes of The Lord of the Rings. It is an epic high fantasy novel written by J. R. R. Tolkien and follows hobbit Frodo Baggins as he and a Fellowship embark on a quest across Middle-earth to destroy the One Ring. It is divided into two books, Book 1 and 2, structured as a modern novel. The Lord of the Rings was initially inspired by the success of Tolkien's earlier work, The Hobbit.
Alan Shepard, Jr. (November 18, 1923 – July 21, 1998) was an American in the United States Navy and later in NASA as an astronaut. He was the first American in space. He went into space on May 5, 1961. He was born in Derry, New Hampshire and died in Pebble Beach, California.

GMA-NMI's products and services include mobile entertainment and digital media, online advertising, and broadband and cable internet services. Aaron Turner (born November 5, 1977) is an American musician, singer, songwriter, and artist best known as a founding member of the metal bands Isis (band) and Old Man Gloom. He also founded the record label Hydra Head Records. Turner is known for his use of complex time signatures and his unique approach to songwriting, which often emphasizes atmosphere and texture over traditional song structures. He has been active in the post-metal scene since the early 1990s.

Harry Carey (born January 16, 1878 – September 21, 1947) was an American actor and one of silent film's earliest superstars. He was one of the first actors to be known by name to the public and was the first cowboy star of the movies. Carey appeared in more than 220 films from 1909 to 1947, including many of director John Ford's early feature films. He is best known for his roles in Western films and his portrayals of Abraham Lincoln.

Agremiação Sportiva Arapiraquense, or simply ASA, is a Brazilian football club from Arapiraca, Alagoas. The club competes in the Campeonato Brasileiro Série C, the third tier of Brazilian football, after winning the 2019 Campeonato Alagoano. ASA was founded on November 8, 1927, and has a membership of approximately 17,000 people.

Aaron Turner (born November 5, 1977) is an American musician, singer, songwriter, and artist best known as a founding member of the metal bands Isis (band) and Old Man Gloom. He also founded the record label Hydra Head Records. Turner is known for his distinctive and artistic approach to heavy music, characterized by his use of complex, interlocking guitar riffs and dense, atmospheric textures. He has been cited as a leading figure in the post-metal genre.

Alan Shepard, Jr. (November 18, 1923 – July 21, 1998) was an American in the Navy, and later in NASA as an astronaut. He was the second person, and the first American, to travel into outer space, and the first American to orbit the Earth. He was born in Derry, New Hampshire, and graduated from the United States Naval Academy at Annapolis, Maryland. He died in Pebble Beach, California of leukemia at age 74.

Aaron Turner (born November 5, 1977) is an American musician, singer, songwriter, and artist best known as a founding member of the metal bands Isis (band) and Old Man Gloom. He also founded the record label Hydra Head Records. Turner is known for his distinctive and artistic approach to heavy music, characterized by his use of complex, interlocking guitar riffs and dense, atmospheric textures. He has also collaborated with a wide range of artists, both in the metal world and beyond, and has released several solo albums that showcase his more experimental and ambient side. Turner was born in Portland, Oregon, and grew up in Massachusetts. He became interested in music as a teenager and played in a number of bands before forming Isis with drummer Aaron Harris in 1997. The band quickly gained a reputation for their innovative and genre-defying sound, which combined elements of metal, post-rock, and shoegaze. They released six studio albums between 1998 and 2010, and toured extensively before disbanding in 2010. Throughout his career, Turner has also been involved in a number of side projects and collaborations. He has played in the bands Old Man Gloom, House of Low Culture, Mamiffer, and Sumac, among others, and has worked with artists like Justin Broadrick, William Fowler Collins, and G. Stuart Dahlquist. In addition to his work as a musician, Turner is also a visual artist and has created album artwork for many of his own projects as well as for other bands. He is known for his distinctive style, which often incorporates intricate, abstract designs and bold, striking imagery. Overall, Aaron Turner is a highly respected and influential figure in the world of heavy music. His innovative approach to guitar playing and his willingness to push the boundaries of the genre have inspired countless musicians, and his work with Isis and other projects continues to be celebrated by fans around the world.

The Velvet Underground's Bootleg Series Volume 1: The Quine Tapes is a live album by The Velvet Underground. It was released in 2001 as a three-CD set on Polydor Records. Expect a Miracle is a compilation album by Brian Kelly, released in 1986. It contains songs from his first two albums, Pools of Light and Afterplay, as well as some new material. The album was well-received by fans and critics alike, showcasing Kelly's unique blend of rock, pop, and folk music. It also features collaborations with other artists, including the hit single "Miracle" featuring John Farnham. Expect a Miracle remains a fan favorite and a testament to Kelly's talent as a musician and songwriter.

Aaron Turner (born October 5, 1977) is an American musician, singer, songwriter, and artist best known as a founding member of the metal bands Isis (band) and Old Man Gloom. He also founded the record label Hydra Head Records. Turner is known for his distinctive and artistic approach to heavy music, characterized by his use of complex, interlocking guitar riffs and dense, atmospheric textures. He has also collaborated with a wide range of artists, both in the metal world and beyond, and has released several solo albums under the name House of Low Culture.

The Velvet Underground were an American rock band formed in New York City in 1964. Their best-known line-up consisted of vocalist/guitarist Lou Reed, keyboardist/vocalist John Cale, guitarist Sterling Morrison, and drummer Maureen Tucker. The band is known for its distinctive sound, which combined Cale's viola playing with Reed's experimental guitar techniques. Their lyrics often dealt with taboo subjects such as drug use, prostitution, and sadomasochism. The band's early albums were not commercially successful, but they have since been recognized as some of the most influential and groundbreaking recordings in the history of popular music.

The Bootleg Series Volume 1: The Quine Tapes is an album by The Velvet Underground. It has a runtime of 230.05 and was recorded in United States, specifically in St. Louis, Missouri. This album belongs to the Rock music genre and was preceded by Squeeze (The Velvet Underground album).
Harry Carey (born January 16, 1878 – September 21, 1947) was an American actor and one of silent films' earliest superstars. He was one of the first actors to be known by his first and last name, and one of the first to draw one-million-dollar salaries. Carey was born in New York City, the son of actors who were touring the country in a theater company. He was raised in the family of his grandmother, who returned with him to New York when he was about ten years old.

Lady Anne Monson, bnita f'in-nofs il- 1723 u mmiet f'in-nofs il- 1774, kienet botanist Brittanika. Kienet zewgta l-governatur tal-Kumpanija tal-Istat Indjan tal-Ingliż, George Monson. Lady Anne kienet interessata f'l-botanika u kkolezzjonat pjanti waqt li kienet ma' marbutha fi l-Indja mal-mexxej tagħha. Kkunsidra l-pjanti li kkolezzjonat bil-ħġarna lill-botanist Svediż, Carl Linnaeus. L-kolezzjoni tal-pjanti tal-Indja tal-Lady Anne kienet waħda mill-aqwa l-ewwel kolezzjonijiet tal-pjanti tal-Indja li ssejħew f'Ewropa.

Darinka Dentcheva, born on January 1, 1958, is an American mathematician who has made significant contributions to the field of mathematical optimization. She received her Ph.D. from the Humboldt University in 1985 and has since been a professor at various universities in the United States. Her research focuses on convex and discrete optimization, as well as their applications in engineering and economics. Dentcheva has been recognized for her work with numerous awards and honors, including the prestigious Fulkerson Prize in 2006.
John McVeagh, a young Irishman, was working as a trader in the South Seas when World War I broke out. He enlisted in the New Zealand Expeditionary Force and took part in the disastrous Gallipoli campaign. After recovering from his wounds, he rejoined his unit in France, where he fought until the end of the war. He then returned to the Pacific.

L-Estádio Municipal Coaracy da Mata Fonseca, li mmiratur f'Arapiraca, hu l-kamp ta' Agremiação Sportiva Arapiraquense. L-iskwadra, li mmiratur wkoll bħala "Agremiação Sportiva Arapiraquense", għandha 17000 membru u qiegħed fil-Campeonato Brasileiro Série C. Il-klabb waqgħet il-kampjonat Campeonato Brasileiro Série C u l-isem kollu tagħhom hu "Agremiação Sportiva Arapiraquense".
Agremiação Sportiva Arapiraquense, commonly known as ASA, is a Brazilian football club based in Arapiraca, Alagoas state. The club competes in the Campeonato Brasileiro Série C, the third tier of Brazilian football, after being relegated from the Série B in 2017. Aaron Turner (born November 5, 1977) is an American musician and artist. He is best known as the guitarist, vocalist, and songwriter for the metal band Isis. He also plays in the related projects House of Low Culture, Old Man Gloom, and Mamiffer. He has also collaborated with Justin Broadrick of Godflesh and Jesu in the band Greymachine. Turner was a member of the post-metal supergroup, Hydra Head Records, and also runs the label, SIGE Records. Turner's primary guitar is a First Act Custom Shop Double Cutaway, which was made for him in 2001. He uses a Fender Twin Reverb Amp.

Louis Levy (28 March 1894 – 1 January 1957) was an English dance band leader and film composer. He was born in London, the son of a furniture maker. He studied at the Royal Academy of Music before going into music publishing. In 1914 he started working for the Aeolian Company, demonstrating their player pianos, and also began making piano rolls for them. In 1916, he started recording for the Columbia Graphophone Company, initially as a pianist, and later as conductor of the Columbia Orchestra. He also recorded for HMV and for Edison Bell's Winner label, often using the pseudonym "Harry S. Pepper" for arrangements of popular songs. He broadcast on radio, and in 1923 was appointed musical director of the Palladium Theatre, where he remained for 17 years.

Alan Shepard, Jr. (November 18, 1923 – July 21, 1998) was an American in the United States Navy and later in NASA as an astronaut. He was born in Derry, New Hampshire. Shepard became the second person to travel into outer space and the first American. He went into space on May 5, 1961. He also went to the Moon on the Apollo 14 mission in 1971. Shepard died of leukemia in Monterey, California at age 74.

Petah Tikva (Hebrew: פֶּתַח תִּקְוַתַּיִם, Arabic: بَتَاه طِقْوَة) is a city in the center of Israel, located in the Tel Aviv District. It is part of the metropolitan area known as Gush Dan. The city was founded in 1878 by a group of Jewish immigrants from Poland. Its name means "Opening of hope" and was inspired by the biblical verse from Hosea 2:15, "I will give her her vineyards from thence, and the valley of Achor for a door of hope".

Bootleg Series Volume 1: The Quine Tapes is an album by the American rock band The Velvet Underground. It was released in 2001 and features recordings made by guitarist Robert Quine during his tenure with the band in the early 1970s. Alan Shepard was born on November 18, 1923, in East Derry, New Hampshire. He received a Bachelor of Science degree from the United States Naval Academy at Annapolis in 1944 and a Master of Arts degree in Aeronautical Engineering from the Naval Postgraduate School in 1957. He also completed the Naval Test Pilot School at Patuxent River, Maryland in 1951. He was one of the Mercury Seven astronauts for NASA. He made his first space flight in May 1961 and made his second space flight as commander of Apollo 14 from January 31 to February 9, 1971. After retiring from NASA and the Navy, he went into private business in Houston, Texas. He died on July 21, 1998, in Pebble Beach, California, from leukemia.

The Lord of the Rings is a film series consisting of three high fantasy adventure films directed by Peter Jackson. They are based on the novel The Lord of the Rings by J. R. R. Tolkien. The films are subtitled The Fellowship of the Ring (2001), The Two Towers (2002) and The Return of the King (2003). The Hobbit is a film series consisting of three epic fantasy adventure films directed by Peter Jackson. It is a prequel to The Lord of the Rings film trilogy. The films are subtitled An Unexpected Journey (2012), The Desolation of Smaug (2013), and The Battle of the Five Armies (2014). J.R.R. Tolkien, born on 3 January 1892, is known for his high fantasy works set in Middle-earth. His most famous works, The Hobbit and The Lord of the Rings, are set in a richly detailed fictional world. The Hobbit, or There and Back Again, is a children's fantasy novel by English author J. R. R. Tolkien. It was published on 21 September 1937 to wide critical acclaim, being nominated for the Carnegie Medal and awarded a prize from the New York Herald Tribune for best juvenile fiction. The story is set in the fictional world of Middle-earth and follows the quest of home-loving hobbit Bilbo Baggins, the titular "hobbit", to win a share of the treasure guarded by Smaug the dragon.

Alan Shepard, li nbidlet l-18 ta’ Novembru, 1923, kien astronaut Amerikan.
Alan Shepard, Jr. (November 18, 1923 – July 21, 1998) was an American in the United States Navy and later in NASA as an astronaut. Shepard was the second person and the first American to travel into outer space. He was born in Derry, New Hampshire. He graduated from the United States Naval Academy at Annapolis in 1947. Shepard died of leukemia in Pebble Beach, California at the age of 74. He won the Distinguished Service Medal.

John Mills (born Lewis Ernest Watts Mills, 22 February 1908 – 23 April 1999) was a British actor who made more than 120 films in a career spanning seven decades. Mills was born in The Watts Naval Training School, North Elmham, Norfolk, England, the son of Edith Mills (née Baksh) and Lewis Mills. He was educated at the Norwich High School for Boys and the Sir John Leman Grammar School in Beccles, Suffolk. He first came to public attention in the late 1920s when he was working for a shipping company in London and was spotted by the actor, producer and director Seymour Hicks, who gave him his first acting job at the Pavilion Theatre in 1929. He made his film debut in 1932 in a quota quickie called The Midshipmaid.

GMA-NMI is based in Quezon City and is responsible for the creation, development and maintenance of the network's new media properties such as the GMA Entertainment Portal (PEP), GMA News Online, GMA on Demand, and GMA Worldwide, Inc.

Aaron Turner, l-artiċlejn li jinsabu magħluq bih, huwa mużikant u artist Amerikan. Huwa aktar magħmul bħala l-għitarist, il-vokalista, u l-kantatur tal-bandi tal-metall ISIS, Old Man Gloom, u Sumac. Turner, bl-istil distintiv tiegħu, jirrangal minn vokalijiet melodjusi bl-iskuża tal-qiegħ, sa l-iskriemmi forti. Turner wkoll qiegħed jinsab notat għall-użu tiegħ tal-bass gitara, spiss jinkludi droni baxxi u linji melodjik tal-bass fil-muxika tiegħ. Turner huwa wieħed mill-qofin tal-Hydra Head Records.

Aaron Turner (born November 5, 1977) is an American musician, singer, songwriter, and artist best known as a founding member of the metal bands Isis (band) and Old Man Gloom. He also founded the record label Hydra Head Records. Turner is known for his distinctive and artistic approach to heavy music, characterized by his use of complex, interlocking guitar riffs and dense, atmospheric textures. He has also collaborated with a wide range of artists, both as a musician and as a visual artist.

Darinka Dentcheva, born on January 1, 1958, is an American mathematician known for her work in stochastic programming and mathematical optimization. She is a professor at the Rutgers University in New Jersey, where she has been a faculty member since 1991. She is also a fellow of the Institute for Operations Research and the Management Sciences (INFORMS).
John Mills (born Lewis Ernest Watts Mills, 22 February 1908 – 23 April 1975) was a Canadian actor. He was born in North Vancouver, British Columbia, and died in London, England. Mills began his career as a child actor in silent films in 1919. He appeared in many British films, and later in American films, as a character actor. He is best known for his role as the village idiot in Ryan's Daughter (1970). He appeared in 123 films between 1921 and 1971.
